               <div class="shareaholic-canvas" data-app="share_buttons" data-app-id="16038450" data-image="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Rh1gGuRR7QU/VPb1123lddI/AAAAAAAAHeA/Ug9FMsDxeHI/s1600/200x200.jpg">
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: justify;">
                <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: large;">

                </span>
               </div>
               <br/>
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                </a>

                 </a>
                 has opened up doors for artists of every stature to partake in their mixtapes and advanced promotions.

               <div style="text-align: justify;">
                <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 They take pride in developing important working relationships with major artists and DJs as well as indie artists that they work with.
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: justify;">
                <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div style="text-align: justify;">
                <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 <i>
                  Devine Jamz Gospel Network
                 </i>
                 commend
                 <a href="http://www.devinebroadcasting.com/#!pookie-wit-tha-uzi/cp62" target="_blank">
                  Adrian "Pookie" Logan
                 </a>
                 for his continuous engagement to spread the Gospel of Jesus in all areas of his life. We are most inspired that he has taken the Gospel to those who need it the most, which are the unbelievers!
                </span>
               </div>
               <br/>
               <i>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      function setAttributeOnload(object, attribute, val) {
      if(window.addEventListener) {
        window.addEventListener('load',
          function(){ object[attribute] = val; }, false);
      } else {
        window.attachEvent('onload', function(){ object[attribute] = val; });
      }
    }
     </script>
